    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText2501277060590525324" style="display:none">They agreed on three months...but their love knew no boundaries.<br /><br />Jack McLachlan is a winemaking magnate and easily one of Australia’s most eligible bachelors. His success and wealth make him no stranger to the complications of romantic relationships and that’s why he goes to extreme measures to avoid the hassle. He prefers simplicity in the form of a beautiful female companion with no strings attached. He arranges relationships like business deals and they’re always the same. No long term relationships. No real names.<br /><br />It’s his game and his rules. He’s content to play as usual, but when Laurelyn Prescott enters his life, his strategy must change because this player is like none he's ever encountered. His world is turned on its head after he begins a three month affair with the beautiful American musician. Nothing goes according to plan and as he breaks more and more of his own rules for her, she’s exceptionally close to becoming something he never thought possible. His ultimate game changer.<br /><br />Not recommended for younger readers due to sexual content and language.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer489035509" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2377378694243539116"><b>
  <i>JUST FUCK ME NOW.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/596253.gif' width='340' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I need the second book like now now now!!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/248667.gif' width='200' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></i>
</b><br/><br/><b>For publishing houses and authors who leave us hanging on the edge of the cliff waiting for the next book...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402561ra/782529.gif' width='340' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> </b><br/><br/>>>>><br/><br/><b>

<div id="review_490408674" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/490408674" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/490408674?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=stalker">stalker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer490408674" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16216415048963306084"><br/>This one just about blew me away. It took me by surprise – I loved every second I was with this book and couldn’t put it down. There’s also a major cliffhanger to leave you desperate for book two.<br/><br/>Well, this one came out of nowhere for me!! What an amazing story – it just blew me away. It totally consumed me – I was engrossed from the first word right through to the very end and, yes, there’s a doozy of a cliffhanger to keep you hanging on for the sequel which is not due out until the summer. How</span>
  <span id="freeText16216415048963306084" style="display:none"><br />This one just about blew me away. It took me by surprise – I loved every second I was with this book and couldn’t put it down. There’s also a major cliffhanger to leave you desperate for book two.<br /><br />Well, this one came out of nowhere for me!! What an amazing story – it just blew me away. It totally consumed me – I was engrossed from the first word right through to the very end and, yes, there’s a doozy of a cliffhanger to keep you hanging on for the sequel which is not due out until the summer. How can I wait that long?? Why?? I need it now!!<br /><br />The Blurb sums it up pretty well – Jack McLachlan, Aussie mutli-millionaire vineyard magnate, arranges his short term ‘relationships’ to avoid emotional attachment. He gets his companions to agree up front to his proposition – he promises them a great time in exchange for a time limit and no real names. Laurelyn, an American girl staying in Australia for 3 months, is perfect. Jack is very attracted to her and she’s got her own expiry date – a ticket back to the USA. She fits the bill beautifully and, after a bit of deliberation and some delicious encouragement from Jack, she agrees to his proposition. So, they assume the identities of Lachlan and Paige, agreeing to 3 months together and the time of their lives.<br /><br />Jack McLachlan – oh, be still my beating heart. I fell hard for this man and I really thought I wouldn’t. I thought he’d be cold, selfish and controlled but he’s not any of that. He’s warm, friendly, loving, caring and very, very sexy. I loved this Aussie and could just hear that delicious accent every time he spoke!! He’s got a big, loving family with a Mum who wants nothing more than to see him happily married with a brood of his own which is exactly why he’s keeping his companions away from her! He’s rich, he’s one of Australia’s most eligible bachelors but he likes to keep his private life very private and he likes to remain in control and set a time limit – no emotional attachment involved.<br /><br />Laurelyn is a lovely heroine – she’s open, engaging, a little bit guarded and she’s about to be swept off her feet by Jack. She knows this relationship has an expiry date and is determined not to fall for him but, the more time they spend together, the deeper she falls, despite her resolution not to care for him. She’s got a dark and troubled past and has just got out of a bad relationship and Jack offers her everything she could ever hope for but with a time limit.<br /><br />They shared some really delicious sex scenes and this erotic, not kinky, and what starts out as just fucking slowly turns into lovemaking and the scene when they are obviously making love for the first time is really very special and had my eyes misting a little. But Jack is determined that this companion, like all the others, is temporary, just number thirteen in a long list and that he will move on after she goes home. He’s also falling deeper and deeper and the ache in his chest when he thinks she won’t be there is becoming ever more painful but will he wake up and see what is right in front of him before it’s too late??<br /><br />Of course, there’s a mother of a cliffhanger that will have you screaming for more! I absolutely loved this and I need the sequel right now!! I really don’t give that fifth star out very often but this is special, a fantastic romance for all of you that love those Fifty Shades style trilogies and it’s only my second 5 star read of 2013 and Jack McLachlan is a new book boyfriend to melt into a puddle for!<br /><br /><b>5 big shiny stars!!</b><br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>Our precious time together feels like a candle with wicks burning at both ends. Once the flame meets in the middle, we’re over. I’ll never see him again, or hear his laugh or touch his skin. I’ll never share a bed with him again. Am I prepared for it when that time comes? I don’t think I am, but it doesn’t matter if I’m not. It’s coming, and I’d better figure out how to get ready.</blockquote>
</b><br /><br /><br /><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>

They have a routine like a couple...<br><br>When they go to Sydney for the Opera Laurelyn doesn't understand why photographers are taking pictures of them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408181i/798342._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jacks father gets rushed to hospital and he takes Laurelyn with him. This is when she finds out the truth... The truth about who he is... But she's not worried. She doesn't care about the money..<br><br>She's more scared because of her feelings for him...<br>The more time she spends with his family, she knows the game has changed, she's fallen in love with him.<br><br>She tells him... While making love.. And he doesn't tell her back.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408181i/798343.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jack is too scared to admit this to himself...     <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3820197-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383385041p2/3820197.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524827316" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13396465667989138236"><br/><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>I read this in one day, starting while having my morning cuppa - <b>
  <i>Bushells</i>
</b> of course - and <b>
  <i>Vegemite</i>
</b> toast for <b>
  <i>brekkie.</i>
</b> Read it through morning <b>
  <i>smoko</i>
</b> with another cuppa and a <b>
  <i>lammie.</i>
</b> On through lunch while eating my <b>
  <i>sanger.</i>
</b> And finished before dinner, which was a good thing as I wasn't sure I could <b>
  <i>bog into</i>
</b> the <b>
  <i>chook</i>
</b> I'd cooked or the <b>
  <i>Tim Tams</i>
</b> for dessert. I'd had my fill of Aussie <b>
  <i>tucker</i>
</b> for the day...<br/><br/>Laurelyn Prescott, an American singer/musician </span>
  <span id="freeText13396465667989138236" style="display:none"><br /><b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br />I read this in one day, starting while having my morning cuppa - <b>
  <i>Bushells</i>
</b> of course - and <b>
  <i>Vegemite</i>
</b> toast for <b>
  <i>brekkie.</i>
</b> Read it through morning <b>
  <i>smoko</i>
</b> with another cuppa and a <b>
  <i>lammie.</i>
</b> On through lunch while eating my <b>
  <i>sanger.</i>
</b> And finished before dinner, which was a good thing as I wasn't sure I could <b>
  <i>bog into</i>
</b> the <b>
  <i>chook</i>
</b> I'd cooked or the <b>
  <i>Tim Tams</i>
</b> for dessert. I'd had my fill of Aussie <b>
  <i>tucker</i>
</b> for the day...<br /><br />Laurelyn Prescott, an American singer/musician has come for a three-month stay with her best friend to Australia. Jack McLachlan, is a wealthy Australian businessman and winegrower. Not one for romantic relationships he sees Laurelyn and knows immediately she's the one he wants to make number thirteen on his list of <i>companions</i>.<br /><br />I did tell myself that I wasn't going to read any more of these <i>FSoG/Bared to You</i> type books. And honestly the only reason I did was because of the setting in Oz and the Australian hero. When almost 99.9% of the books I read are set anywhere <i>but</i> in Australia, one set in Oz <b>
  <i>and</i>
</b> with an Australian hero certainly piques my interest.<br /><br />Initially the hero comes across as a predatory sleaze, lying-in-wait for his next victim. It's not an attractive introduction. However as the story moves along and we get to know him - especially his family - he improves. <br /><br />The author, obviously not Australian, tried hard to make Jack's parts sound authentic. But she did tend to overdo the Australian-isms - <i>see first paragraph above</i> - although I doubt anyone but the locals would notice. We don't use the term <i>'pumps'</i> for high-heeled shoes or <i>'ass'</i> it's <i>arse.</i> <i>'Panties'</i> are <i>undies</i> and <i>'Mom'</i> is <i>Mum</i> - although she did get that one right most of the time. Just those little things - and there were a number of them - that drew me out of the story.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Cliffie Alert!!</i>
</b><br />Yep, another one. So, be warned.<br /><br />Bottom line. If you <i>still</i> haven't had your fill of the billionaire businessman à la Christian Grey, Gideon Cross, et al, then this will suit you. One of its strengths is that the setting and hero are different to the usual. Even though for me it started off weakly with too much of the same ole, same ole, it did get better the longer I read and the hero became way more appealing. Pity about his douchie beginning.<br /><br /><b>Steam:</b> 3.5<br /><br /></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_523797593" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/523797593" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/523797593?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer523797593" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17805644423562637013"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407752i/796823._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote> <b> <i> “Baby, you’ve fucked with my mind without touching my body.” </i></b>
</blockquote>  <br/><b> Pure escapism. An engaging, entertaining multi-millionaire romance. </b><br/><br/>It wasn’t a very emotional read for me but it did keep me turning the pages straight through the night till the sun came up <br/><br/>I definitely got some Fifty Shades/Blackstone vibes off of this book (it was hot, but just straight vanilla, no kinky fuckery), so if you’re a fan of those, you should check this out for sure.<br/><br/>When Laurelyn goes to Australia for 3 months wit</span>
  <span id="freeText17805644423562637013" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407752i/796823._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> <i> “Baby, you’ve fucked with my mind without touching my body.” </i></b>
</blockquote>  <br><b> Pure escapism. An engaging, entertaining multi-millionaire romance. </b><br><br>It wasn’t a very emotional read for me but it did keep me turning the pages straight through the night till the sun came up <br><br>I definitely got some Fifty Shades/Blackstone vibes off of this book (it was hot, but just straight vanilla, no kinky fuckery), so if you’re a fan of those, you should check this out for sure.<br><br>When Laurelyn goes to Australia for 3 months with her best friend, the last thing she was looking for was a relationship.<br><br>Meanwhile, Jack was actively searching for one. But… he wasn’t looking for a conventional relationship. He was looking for the right woman to share his bed for no longer than 3 months. A no-strings attached companionship at the end of which both parties would walk away. The moment he sees Laurelyn, he knew she was it.<br><br>But… to complicate matters, he insisted on personal secrecy. No names, no connections, no attachments.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “My life is complicated for reasons I won’t discuss. When it comes to dating I need it to be simple and undemanding. Disclosing my identity complicates things, so you wouldn’t know my real name.”<br><br>“You’re not joking.”<br><br>I can’t read her reaction. I have no idea if she’s on board or freaking out. “When the three months is over, so are we. I’ll move on and you will too. Because you won’t know my name or any identifying information about me, you’ll have no way to contact me. Ever.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>And despite her initial hesitation, Laurelynn agrees and then it really became a question of them being able to get through the 3 months and not stay attached…<br><br>I have to say that despite my liking him from the start, Jack’s aloofness and secrecy kept me from fully connecting with him until later in the story. I guess it bothered me a little how detatched he kept trying to be. But the more we found out about him, the more I began to understand his motivations.<br><br>The heroine just plain rocked. I connected with her nearly instantly. I loved that she was constantly one upping him, putting little cracks in his facade and not just instantly swooning into his arms.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “The three months we spend together would be the best of your life. You’d never be able to top what you’d experience with me.”<br><br>She sits back and laughs. “Well at least you’re not egotistical.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>I liked that the story was told in alternating POVs and I especially found that, given how much of a mystery Jack was, getting to see his train of thought was helpful in understanding the motivations behind his demands, actions and choices.<br><br>One thing I really loved about Jack was that, temporary relationship or not, he didn’t tolerate stupid things getting in between them. There was one incident in particular which as soon as it happened, I rolled my eyes expecting chapters of stupidity back and forth but was SO pleased that the moment he understood what was happening, he just made a call that cleared everything up quickly and efficiently and put an end to the drama. I was really impressed with him at that point.<br><br>This book built slowly but steadily with no slow spots and kept me engaged throughout. <br><br>I liked it all along but it wasn’t until the end that I really fell in love with it. Now, this IS romance so we all know going in that at some point, the hero was going to admit that he was smitten with the heroine but I guess what was holding a part of me back until the end was that, despite knowing that he would eventually get to that point, I wasn’t sure I wanted to give my heart over to falling in love a guy who seemed so willing to walk away. That said, I loved how by the end he really truly realized what he was losing and it was at that point that I began to really fall in love.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “Don’t leave. I want you to be with me.” … I swallow before I say the words that will change this relationship forever. “You’re the one I need.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>I love that they finally reached the point where the pretense of their relationship being temporary was over and now I’m hoping the focus will be on them building something together.<br><br>There is a HUGE cliffhanger (but it was one that we saw coming right from the beginning) and I can’t wait to see what book #2 has in store for Jack and Laurelynn!<br><br>4 stars<br><br>Beauty From Surrender (Beauty #2) will be released on May 30, 2013.<br><br><i> My casting.... <br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407752i/796824._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407752i/796825._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1360699932l/17156015.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> They agreed on three months...but their love knew no boundaries.<br><br>Jack McLachlan is a winemaking magnate and easily one of Australia’s most eligible bachelors. His success and wealth make him no stranger to the complications of romantic relationships and that’s why he goes to extreme measures to avoid the hassle. He prefers simplicity in the form of a beautiful female companion with no strings attached. He arranges relationships like business deals and they’re always the same. No long term relationships. No real names.<br><br>It’s his game and his rules. He’s content to play as usual, but when Laurelyn Prescott enters his life, his strategy must change because this player is like none he's ever encountered. His world is turned on its head after he begins a three month affair with the beautiful American musician. Nothing goes according to plan and as he breaks more and more of his own rules for her, she’s exceptionally close to becoming something he never thought possible. His ultimate game changer. </i><br><br>Not recommended for younger readers due to sexual content and language.<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17805644423562637013" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_569975065" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/569975065" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/569975065?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781301550753" href="/book/show/17570661-beauty-from-pain">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=lendable">lendable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=battle-of-the-books-2013">battle-of-the-books-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-a-h">authors-a-h</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer569975065" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer615577577811391047">I am thrilled to have discovered Georgia Cates – wow - I absolutely loved Beauty from Pain and can’t wait to read more of her books.<br/><br/>As a romantic addict, this book had everything I love in a story – beautiful characters that I immediately “bond” with, romance, amazing sex, loss, pain, magnificent locations, fabulous plot and great writing. <br/><br/>Beautiful and talented Laurelyn Prescott is in Australia with her best friend to get over a broken relationship and to sort things out in her life and the las</span>
  <span id="freeText615577577811391047" style="display:none">I am thrilled to have discovered Georgia Cates – wow - I absolutely loved Beauty from Pain and can’t wait to read more of her books.<br><br>As a romantic addict, this book had everything I love in a story – beautiful characters that I immediately “bond” with, romance, amazing sex, loss, pain, magnificent locations, fabulous plot and great writing. <br><br>Beautiful and talented Laurelyn Prescott is in Australia with her best friend to get over a broken relationship and to sort things out in her life and the last thing she wants is getting involved with anyone.<br><br>Jack Henry McLachlan, is rich, sexy and gorgeous and one of Australia’s most eligible playboys, who does not do “love” or “relationships”, preferring to have very short and anonymous liaisons.<br><br>When he first sees Laurelyn, he decides that she’s going to be his “next” ONE. <br><br>When the two finally get together, after a lot of “sneaky” manipulation on Jack’s part,, he proposes that they have a 3 month relationship with no strings attached. After that period, both will walk away with no regrets.<br><br>Though she has some misgivings about it, she finds him totally irresistible and eventually agrees to his proposal.<blockquote>
  <b>“If I do this, something will go wrong and this man will hurt me. I know it as sure as I’m sitting here next to him feeling how much he makes me want to say yes.”</b>
</blockquote>What Jack soon realizes is that Laurelyn is nothing like the women he has ever been with. She’s open, funny, and sexy and has something that gets under his skin, having you doing things that he has never done with other women. <br><br>I loved seeing how Jack &amp; Laurelyn's relationship developed, their banter, <br><blockquote>
  <b>“My lasagne has been known to bring me to the knees."<br>"Baby, it doesn’t take food for you to bring me to my knees.”</b>
</blockquote>Their emotional connection, their friendship, and sexual tension. The “sex” scenes were incredibly sensual and so sexy and so hot. <br><br>I adored these two – Jack, faced with feelings and emotions he has never experienced before, suddenly begins to think that he may want more than his original proposal to Laurelyn. He’s such a fabulous guy…how could anyone resist this gorgeous man????<blockquote>
  <b>“Don’t leave. I want you to be with me.”<br>“You’ll have your family.”<br>I swallow before I say the words that will change this relationship forever. “You’re the one I need.”<br>“But that would mean meeting your family.”<br>It does, and I’m okay with that if it means she’s by my side. “I don’t care. I need you to be with me.”<br>She smiles and cradles my face with her hands. “Of course. I’ll come if it’s what you want, but this is going to change everything.”<br>“I know, but it’s what I want.”</b>
</blockquote>And Laurelyn – I loved her….she was someone so special…despite a horrible childhood, a flaky mom, betrayals in her life is still open to the possibilities of life…love, caring, sharing. <br>Did I ever think that Jack could resist her and not fall in love???? Never. This was meant to be <blockquote>
  <b>“She has bewitched me. And I want her. She’s the one.” <br><br>“I love her too much to let her leave and I need to tell her right this minute.”</b>
</blockquote>….why the hell did you let her go???? <br><br>I ‘bawled” my eyes out when I read Laurelyn’s goodbye note!!!!!!!!! “Please don’t go” I shouted ….<br><br>There’s such an incredible sense of family and friends in this story. Jack's loving family, his housekeeper, Laurelyn’s mother (I will always think of her when I hear Jolene!!!), Addison, her "wacky" friend.<br><br>Great dialogue filled with fabulous one-liners , good humor and so much more.<blockquote>
  <b>“Liar, liar. My pants are so on fire. And so is the rest of me.”</b>
</blockquote>The settings were really great. Australia wine farms, exciting cities, and small towns. Loved it.<br><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414691i/817894.jpg" alt=" photo 3f2bc0224665c823e03cec302df72fff_zpsdb315b8a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br>I was a bit apprehensive about the 2 POV’s but I found that I really liked it. You get into both characters thoughts and feelings which is great.<br><br>THE QUOTE I LOVED THE MOST<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Nothing speaks louder than your heart. Listen to what it's telling you.”</b>
</blockquote>I read this book NON-STOP. I couldn’t put it down. I am so invested in the story and Jack &amp; Laurelyn that I can’t wait for the next “part” of their love story – which it is ….an amazing LOVE STORY.<br><br>And….WHAT A STUNNING, AMAZING, BEAUTIFUL COVER!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="615577577811391047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5753312581396354712" style="display:none"><b>4 Love, agreements and so many feelings Stars<br><br><i>They agreed to three months...<br>But their love knew no boundaries.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399957ra/774514.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Australia's multimillionaire and most eligible bachelor <b>Jack Henry McLachlan</b> meets young American aspiring singer <b>Laurelyn Prescott</b> he thinks he found his 13th companion. No feelings, no strings attached. It's lust pure and simple. He propositions a 3 month relationship without even exchanging names. He will be Lachlan and she will be Paige and they will enjoy each other, freely and uncomplicated.<br><br><b>
  <i>“When the three months is over, so are we. I'll move on and you will too. Because you won't know my name or any identifying information about me, you'll have no way to contact me. Ever.”</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407707i/796636.jpg" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But what begins easy and carefree, will turn passionate and one of a kind. It will grow into a love that Jack is reluctant to admit and Laurelyn so ready to give. When the time will come for her to return home will Jack fight to keep her where she belongs? With him. And Laurelyn will stay and prove to them both that they are above arrangements and simple sex or this one more blow will shatter her damaged heart?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407707i/796637.gif" width="364" height="74" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sometimes when love is involved the lines between facade and reality blur and you become invested in the other. You care more than you wished and you've ever hoped for. And in the most unexpected place you find the other half of your soul. And you know it when you lose it.<br><br><b>
  <i>You made my every fantasy come<br>true and that includes finding the love of my life. Now, it’s my turn to keep my promise.<br>I love you, Jack Henry, with every fiber of my being. Forever.<br>Laurelyn<br>Your American girl.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/609011.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>But I did fall in love with her, and now she’s gone.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/619592.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I’ve known pain my whole life, but this is a new kind for me. It isn’t born of something wrong or ugly. This pain is conceived out of beauty—my love for Jack Henry McLachlan. I embrace it. I clutch it as tightly as I can with both fists because I never want to forget the love I have for him. Loving him will forever be my Beauty from Pain.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/593067.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><pre>HOW ON EARTH TO EXPLAIN ALL THESE FEELINGS?</pre><br><br>Passionate, engaging, exciting, hot and enticing this is A GREAT READ! But my feelings are certainly complicated and I am all heartbroken, furious and in love...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406966ra/794505.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First we have another book about an arrangement. You would think I had enough of contracts by now to begin an exciting (NOT!) career as lawyer, but I am sucker for emotionally damaged heroes with redeeming qualities. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407707i/796638.jpg" width="400" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407707ra/796639.gif" width="400" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course I wanted to bash Jack's head in! He was arrogant and infuriating, hardheaded and just plain stupid. He made me angry and he broke my heart with his inability to trust and he made me swoon because who am I kidding, he is DELICIOUS!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407707ra/796640.gif" width="400" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He doesn't realise the treasure that he holds until the bitter end and even then you can't stay mad at him for long. Because he is finally awake and you hope that all will work out.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407707ra/796641.gif" width="400" height="173" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But they don't... Because it is a book and there is a sequel and you just lay there hugging your Kindle and sobbing and staring at the ceiling and you pray that these two stupid ostriches will pull their heads out of <s>their asses</s>... ehmm the SAND and will realise that you can't deny love!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407707ra/796642.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the way their hearts beat for each other...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407707i/796643.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Starting the next with my heart full of stars and hope and wishes for a grovel to end all grovels... Yes, Jack darling I am talking to you!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/473732.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/480907539?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2012</a>

        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480907539" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9222547150530789596"><b>4.5 Ah-mazing Jacktastic Stars!!! </b><br/><br/>What would you say if a handsome man in a foreign country wanted to have a no strings attached 3 month relationship with you? You wouldn’t know each others real identities, there would be no pretenses, no exceptions and he promises to make all your fantasies come true? What if he had an Australian accent and looked like this guy?<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207135i/23997202.jpg' width='400' height='540' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>Jack McLachlan </b><br/><i>I sit in the dark corner and can the room like a starved predator searching for prey. I haven’t chosen her yet, but the</i></span>
  <span id="freeText9222547150530789596" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Ah-mazing Jacktastic Stars!!! </b><br><br>What would you say if a handsome man in a foreign country wanted to have a no strings attached 3 month relationship with you? You wouldn’t know each others real identities, there would be no pretenses, no exceptions and he promises to make all your fantasies come true? What if he had an Australian accent and looked like this guy?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207135i/23997202.jpg" width="400" height="540" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Jack McLachlan </b><br><i>I sit in the dark corner and can the room like a starved predator searching for prey. I haven’t chosen her yet, but the woman who will share my bed for the next few months is sitting in this room right now.</i><br>When I read Jacks first line in this book^ I thought he seemed like a bit of a creeper, let me assure you- he is not! Jack leads a very private life without long term relationships. He is one of the wealthiest eligible bachelors in Australia, and he is not interested in settling down with someone who is interested in publicity or his finances. He is on the prowl for his new ‘flavor of the month’ when he see’s Laurelyn at a local bar performing. He notices her right away and gets information on her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207135i/23997203.jpg" width="330" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Laurelyn is on a three month vacation with her best friend Addison. They are staying with Addi’s brother Ben. Laurelyn needs some time away from her life in Nashville, she is a musician so she can easily get away for a while. She notices Jack in the bar, and is surprised to see him at a wine event she goes to the next night.<br><br> Jack asks her to dinner, and she accepts. While at dinner, Jack or ‘Lauchlan’ explains his situation to Laurelyn and gives her the proposal. At first, she denies quickly. It just doesn’t feel right to her. But the more she thinks about it...<br><b>Whatever the cause, I’m damaged goods. Maybe I should consider this. It’s not like I have a better offer on the table.</b><br> And after this advice from her best friend Addison, <br><b>
  <i> “The best way to get over somebody is to get under someone else.”</i>
</b><br>She accepts. <br>Lauchlan and Laurelyn get a long well, and have great chemistry. But the question is still out there... <br><b>
  <i>“How can you think its possible to have something this hot without one of us getting burned?”</i>
</b><br><br>As their arrangement goes on, the couple spend more time together and learn more about each other. Laurelyn shows Lauchlan her favorite form of exercise (wow) and Lauchlan basically asks Laurelyn to move in, even though the other ‘arrangements’ had never been to his home. Laurelyn sings for Lauchlan- they start to develop more of a relationship than either of them want to admit. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207135i/23997200.jpg" width="400" height="340" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> There are still secrets between them. Until one night, when Lauchlan has a family emergency, some things come to light and things change. <br><b>The game has changed. The rules are no longer the same, but I don’t have the manual. He does, and I need guidance on where to go from here. </b><br><br>Time is running out for these two to be together. They are both developing feelings they aren’t sure what to do with, and Laurelyn is doing something she never wanted to do. She is falling in love. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207135i/23997201.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Laurelyn has some issues from her past, but she is still able to open up with Jack and tell him things about her self that she’s never told anyone else. She knows their arrangement has an expiration date, but she can’t help falling for him. <br><br>Jack Henry McLachlan... He was protective, a bit possessive, and very very sexy! <br><b>
  <i>“I’m going to get you in my bed so I can show you all the ways I can make you come.”</i>
</b> <i>Umm.... yes, please and thank you.</i><br>He also had a sensitive, sweet, and kind side. He was always doing nice things for Laurelyn, and treated her well. <br><b>
  <i>“You treat me like I’m somebody instead of a nobody.”<br>“You’re such a special person. You should always be treated like somebody.”</i>
</b><br>A swoon-worthy man- for sure! <br><br>I will talk a bit about the end... there is a cliffhanger- I know, I know, they suck. I have been reading a ton go them lately... but don’t let that stop you from reading this one! I am so excited for the second book, and at the end of this story, you get a sneak peak of book 2, which makes the cliffy ending not so bad!  <br><br>Beauty from Pain surprised me in the best way! I didn’t have many expectations for this book, but I really loved it! The story was fantastic, the characters were great, and it had some sexy scenes. It was just overall an awesome read!<br><br><b>
  <i>The pain is conceived out of beauty- my love for Jack Henry McLachlan. I embrace it. I clutch it as tightly as I can with both fists because I never what to forget the love I have for him. Loving him will forever be my <u>Beauty from Pain</u>.</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_524037566" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/524037566" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524037566?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17337340-beauty-from-pain">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=steamy-romance">steamy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524037566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14840671634366677901"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407784i/796893.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>I sit in the dark corner and scan the room like a starved predator searching for prey. I haven't chosen her yet, but the woman who will share my bed for the next few months is in this room right now.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407784i/796894.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>He has the ability to weaken my knees, and my body is no longer my own to control. It belongs to him, to do with as he wishes. He's my puppeteer.</i>
</b><br/><br/>I had a tough time rating this book, because as much as I liked certain parts of it, some parts of it just down right did not work for me.<br/><br/>We have Jack H</span>
  <span id="freeText14840671634366677901" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407784i/796893.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>I sit in the dark corner and scan the room like a starved predator searching for prey. I haven't chosen her yet, but the woman who will share my bed for the next few months is in this room right now.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407784i/796894.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He has the ability to weaken my knees, and my body is no longer my own to control. It belongs to him, to do with as he wishes. He's my puppeteer.</i>
</b><br><br>I had a tough time rating this book, because as much as I liked certain parts of it, some parts of it just down right did not work for me.<br><br>We have Jack Henry McLachlan, a multimillionaire that is looking to find a woman to have an "arrangement" with. All he wants is no-strings attached sex for a few months, nothing else. When he sees American beauty, Laurelyn, perform at a club while on her visit to Australia, he's just got to have her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407784i/796895.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and if I'm being perfectly honest here?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407784ra/796896.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now don't get me wrong, I still enjoyed this book. After the 40% mark, I read it straight through to the end in one sitting, staying up to do it. So that's gotta tell you something.<br><br>I think that the whole set-up of a multimillionaire meets the poor girl and offers up his "arrangement" to her just irritated me in the beginning. Thankfully there was no contract involved in this one, or I might have had to throw something, like my kindle, at the wall.<br><br>It took me a while to warm up to Jack. I think the fact that he didn't even want to exchange real names just came off as a bit creepy to me in the beginning. <br><br>I did come to understand why he would do that further into the book, but it was hardly endearing in the beginning.<br><br>There was also the fact that during Laurelyn's internal monologue, she referred to her....well....as "slut button" and "pleasureland". I might have had a giggle...or five...from that.<br><br>I also had a hard time believing how a girl with Laurelyn's history, would agree to an arrangement like that, but I suppose now I'm just also being nitpicky, so I'll move on to the things that I liked.<br><br>Jack Henry, once I moved on past my somewhat iffy first impression of him, was hot. The man is pure sex on a stick.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407784ra/796897.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The sex between him and Laurelyn, though quite frequent, was very hot, and not repetitive. Who can't appreciate an Aussie hottie with a penchant for going down under? Did I also mention he has possessive tendencies?<br><blockquote>
  <i>"You're mine. Do you understand?"<br>"Yes!" I scream partly because it's my answer, but mostly because what he's doing feels so good.<br>"I want you to say it."<br>We're sideways on the bed and each thrust shoves me farther across the mattress until my head is hanging off the edge. "I'm...yours...and...no...one...else's."<br>"No one else touches you here like this."<br>I'm panting as I lift my hips against him and his fingers. "Only you, Lachlan."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Though Laurelyn enjoys their "relationship", she also doesn't have any delusions on what it really is.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>I'm on my back and I stare up at the beautiful sheer panels draped over the canopy above us with one thought- this bed was meant for making love, but that isn't what we just did. It never is.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Laurelyn was a character that I really enjoyed. Even given her history of "daddy issues", she was a very endearing and strong character. I loved that she pole danced for exercise. The scene in the gym when she danced for Jack was not one I will ever be forgetting.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407784ra/796898.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Baby you've fucked my mind without touching my body."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I judge a book by my ability to put it down. The second half of this book left me unable to put it down at all until I finished. That says something.<br><br>I was, however, left with a few questions when it ended. I still do not understand Jack's reactions to the possibility of children. <br>I also wish we were given a little more background into his relationship history, since I was left wondering why one of his ex "arrangements" was the only one that knew his real name. I wish we were given a little more information there. That might have explained some of Audrey's psycho reactions. As it was, I was left feeling like she was just inserted into the story for additional drama.<br><br>I'm hoping that the second book might delve into this a little more and give us just a little bit more of Jack's background.<br><br>As much as I enjoyed this book, the few issues that I had left me from giving this 5 stars. I'm very stingy with my 5 star ratings, I reserve those for the books that I absolutely LOVED. Now while this was not one of those books for me, I still enjoyed it thoroughly.<br><br>There is a cliffhanger at the end, so I would recommend having both books on hand and reading the second right after.<br><br>So I will go with something between 3 and 4 stars...3.75</span>
  <a data-text-id="14840671634366677901" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_780184958" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/780184958" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/780184958?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cotton-candy-romance">cotton-candy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-alpha-syndrome">the-alpha-syndrome</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer780184958" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2118830847964867776"> <b>4,5 Secretive Stars!</b><br/><br/>Winemaker Jack and aspirant-singer Laurelyn met when she’s spending a three month vacation in Australia, they have no idea what they’re getting into. <br/>I mean… they do, but they would never predict the outcome of their little “arrangement”. <br/>Jack only do no-strings-attached relationships, where they both know exactly what they’re getting out of it, where neither of them know their real names and in the end they take different paths and never hear of the other again. And so far,</span>
  <span id="freeText2118830847964867776" style="display:none"> <b>4,5 Secretive Stars!</b><br><br>Winemaker Jack and aspirant-singer Laurelyn met when she’s spending a three month vacation in Australia, they have no idea what they’re getting into. <br>I mean… they do, but they would never predict the outcome of their little “arrangement”. <br>Jack only do no-strings-attached relationships, where they both know exactly what they’re getting out of it, where neither of them know their real names and in the end they take different paths and never hear of the other again. And so far, that would never had been a problem for him. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388799837i/7932732.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But as the time passes and things progress, masks get harder to keep and secrets get harder to keep. <br>There are some relationships that come with strings no matter how free we want them, and as they find out that sometimes feelings grow even when we want them to remain purely physical and fight against it, they are already too late and too tied up. <br>But things aren’t always straight and easy and when are secrets, dark pasts and old sins in the way… even the freest relationship can come with a price. And a high one. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388799837i/7932733.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book surprised me in a really good way. It’s fresh and it has some aspects that make it more original than other books of the genre. <br>I loved both characters and although I’d got annoyed at some points it engaged me from the beginning. I can’t wait for the next book.<br>Definitely a series to have on watch! ;) <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating:</b> 4,5 stars<br> <b>Storyline:</b> A pretty common plot of rich-playboy meets girl and only want no-strings-attached relationship but end up wanting more. But with some twists that make it more original.<br> <b>Writing Style:</b> Fresh and Engaging. First person. Dual POV.<br> <b>Character Development: </b>	 Pretty good. Their connection felt very real and I ended up rooting for them as if I knew them in real life.<br> <b>Steam: </b> Very good with hot moments. Some pretty sweet either. <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Cliffhanger. But it’s part of a series so I’m expecting a HEA in the end.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_522749730" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/522749730" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/522749730?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522749730" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13763932346437329808">4 1/2- 5 stars. I just finished this book and I have these lyrics running through my head:<br/><p>
  <i>Once upon time<br/> A few mistakes ago<br/> I was in your sights<br/> You got me alone<br/> You found me<br/> You found me<br/> You found me<br/> <br/> I guess you didn't care<br/> And I guess I liked that<br/> And when I fell hard<br/> You took a step back<br/> Without me, without me, without me<br/><br/> And he's long gone<br/> When he's next to me<br/> And I realize the blame is on me<br/><br/> Cause I knew you were trouble when you walked in<br/> So shame on me now<br/> Flew me to places i'd never </i></p></span>
  <span id="freeText13763932346437329808" style="display:none">4 1/2- 5 stars. I just finished this book and I have these lyrics running through my head:<br><p>
  <i>Once upon time<br> A few mistakes ago<br> I was in your sights<br> You got me alone<br> You found me<br> You found me<br> You found me<br> <br> I guess you didn't care<br> And I guess I liked that<br> And when I fell hard<br> You took a step back<br> Without me, without me, without me<br><br> And he's long gone<br> When he's next to me<br> And I realize the blame is on me<br><br> Cause I knew you were trouble when you walked in<br> So shame on me now<br> Flew me to places i'd never been<br> So you put me down oh<br> I knew you were trouble when you walked in<br> So shame on me now<br> Flew me to places i'd never been<br> Now i'm lying on the cold hard ground<br> Oh, oh, trouble, trouble, trouble<br> Oh, oh, trouble, trouble, trouble<br><br> No apologies<br> He'll never see you cry<br> Pretend he doesn't know<br> That he's the reason why<br> You're drowning, you're drowning, you're drowning…<i></i></i>
</p><p><br>Book 2 where are you?? Sarcasm inserted here:<br><br>I had a dream last night….. <br></p><p>
  <i>I'm reading a book that is a stand-alone single book that has that elusive Happily Ever After.<br><i></i></i>
</p><p>….<br><br>Then I wake up.<br><br></p><p>
  <b>Another Mother-effing @$#%&amp;^%$ cliffhanger!<b></b></b>
</p><p><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371663ra/724790.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Sadistic authors. They do so love to torture. My frustration is in direct proportion to how good this book is. Way up there. This is my first read by this author and I can already tell you I will be checking out her other books…yes I know, I am a masochist. Sue me. <br> This book starts out with Jack McLachlan, (aka Lachlan aka Jack Henry) sitting in a bar on the hunt for his next prey. He is selfish, calculating, and unapologetic about it. His m.o. is finding agreeable women to have a purely sexual relationship for an agreed upon amount of time where they know nothing about each other. Not even their real names. Usually these only last a few weeks but he is ready to find someone to use for 3 months this time. Then they part and never contact each other again. Well, he's about to be in for a rude awakening. And her name is Laurelyn. <br> Laurelyn is visiting Australia with her best friend for 3 months and escaping from a painful history in order to make some big life choices. She's a talented musician, honest, funny, and beautiful. The whole package. Love her. She meets Jack her first night there and Jack pursues her ruthlessly to agree to his "deal". <br> The more time they spend together, the more rules Jack wants to break with Laurelyn. She blows him away with her sweetness, vulnerability, honesty, and sexiness. How can he give her up? He's determined to do just that. Stubborn man. We see a metamorphosis from detached and selfish to affectionate, possessive, and battling his feelings with every step. Laurelyn brings him to his knees (literally) and as the end of their three months approaches, they both come to realize that this relationship is so far from what they planned it's in another hemisphere. <br> This book kept me on edge, smiling, laughing, and cursing. Loved the fact that it was set in Australia. I've read quite a bit of Brit Lit but this was new for me and I loved learning some Aussie slang. ( sanger for brekkie anyone?) <br> This is a fabulous book and I will definitely be picking up book two this summer.</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="13763932346437329808" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5511993591547605087" style="display:none"><b>Cheers to Lucky Number 13! </b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407796i/796953._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Laurelyn Prescott, an up and coming musician, arrives in Australia with her best friend, Addison to spend the next three months away from her life in Nashville, Tennessee. Seeing the beautiful southern belle and hearing her sing, Jack is hell bent on making her his number 13.<br> <br>Jack Henry has never let any of the prior 12 woman know his real name, or where he lives and absolutely never lets his family meet them. All of these things happen with Laurelyn.<br> <br>During the three months the two learn about each other and engage in a seriously hot sexual relationship. All the while the reality of what will happen at the end of the three months looms over them. Laurelyn had awoken a part of Jack that he may not have known existed. <br> <br><b><i>”A part of me wants Laurelyn to leave so I can go back to my life before her, but then there’s another part that wants to beg her to stay forever. As hard as I try, I can’t decide which is stronger.” ~ </i>Jack </b><br><br>A reader is never at a loss as to where the characters hearts and heads are as the story is told in alternating povs. <br><br>I found the cliffhanger ending to be predictable but I enjoyed the journey nonetheless. <br> <br><b><i>The pain is conceived out of beauty- my love for Jack Henry McLachlan. I embrace it. I clutch it as tightly as I can with both fists because I never what to forget the love I have for him. Loving him will forever be my Beauty from Pain.” ~ </i>Laurelyn</b><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer630154113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6098756108488108117"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 Smoking Hot Jack Henry Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844398._SY540_.jpg' height='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>They agreed to three months...<br/>But their love knew no boundaries.<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844399._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Laurelyn Prescott needs to get away from Nashville for a while, because things at home are not going well. She decides to accompany her best friend Addison to Austrailia on a three month vacation, where they will stay at Addison's brother, Ben's apartment. Laurelyn isn't looking </span>
  <span id="freeText6098756108488108117" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 Smoking Hot Jack Henry Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844398._SY540_.jpg" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>They agreed to three months...<br>But their love knew no boundaries.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844399._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Laurelyn Prescott needs to get away from Nashville for a while, because things at home are not going well. She decides to accompany her best friend Addison to Austrailia on a three month vacation, where they will stay at Addison's brother, Ben's apartment. Laurelyn isn't looking for anything while she's there, but Addison insists she should try to get together with Ben. Unfortunately, she's just not interested. Things start to change when she meets Jack McLachlan.<br><br>Jack McLachlan is a successful wealthy winemaking magnate. He is well-known in Australia, and that is why he likes to lead a very private life. That means long lasting relationships are a big no-no for him. He doesn't want anything complicated. He only does simple, short, anonymous, no strings attatched affairs. And that is exactly what he was in search for when he meets Laurelyn Prescott. He knows he has found the one for what he has in mind. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844399._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I started this book and I was <b>completely</b> hooked from the get-go. I <b>didn't</b> want to put this down. I'm <b>not</b> gonna lie. I found Jack McLachlan to be <b>very</b> intriguing.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844400._SY540_.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, it starts with Laurelyn's arrival to <b>Wagga Wagga, Australia</b>, where she pretty much has to <b>avoid</b> her best friend's brother Ben, as much as possible. Ben <b>doesn't</b> get the hint that she is just <b>not</b> into him. They all go to a <b>bar</b> on her first night there. Laurelyn is a twenty-two year old <b>musician, singer, and songwriter</b>, so, when she sees it's karaoke night, she goes on stage and <b>sings</b>. This is where twenty-nine year old Jack McLachlan sees her. He is <b>captivated</b> by her presence on stage and all he knows is he <b>has</b> to meet her.<br><br>The <b>attraction</b> between these two is <b>definitely</b> there, as well as the <b>sexual tension</b>. After he discovers she will be staying in Australia for <b>three months</b>, and then go back home to America after that, he knows that she is indeed <b>perfect</b>. The <b>ending</b> will be clean and he will <b>never</b> risk bumping into her again. Now, all Jack has to do is <b>proposition</b> her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“When the three months is over, so are we. I'll move on and you will too. Because you won't know my name or any identifying information about me, you'll have no way to contact me. Ever."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I’m a very wealthy man. The three months we spend together would be the best of your life. You’d never be able to top what you’d experience with me... I'd make your fantasies a reality.” <br><br>"Sounds like you need an escort or a prostitute, and I'm neither of those things."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>I <b>loved</b> the fact that she wasn't the <b>typical</b> heroine that falls for the guy and goes off with him <b>blindly</b>. She stood up <b>for</b> herself and thought <b>alot</b> about it before coming to a decision. I was <b>so</b> glad about that. I <b>liked</b> her from then on and was <b>really</b> able to connect with her.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844401._SY540_.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jack was <b>SO FREAKING HOT!</b> Okay,<b>*deep breath*</b> I needed to let that out. Anyways, he was <b>possessive, sexy</b> and just plain <b>Awesome</b>, oh yeah, and he has an Australian accent <b>*Swoon*</b>. He <b>melted</b> my panties so many times. We were able to see his <b>POV</b>, as well as Laurelyn's. I absolutely <b>loved</b> that! I love getting to see what is going on in the hero's <b>mind</b>, because then I get to <b>understand</b> him better. I very much enjoyed the <b>steaminess</b> he brought to the story and seeing him slowly <b>fall</b> for Laurelyn.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>She makes me want to break down and tell her everything. It’s strange -- I’ve never wanted to do that before. She makes me want to do lots of new things.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>They both had <b>a lot</b> of things to get over. Laurelyn has things in her <b>past</b> that have deeply <b>affected</b> her. While Jack has <b>trust</b> issues and <b>doesn't</b> let anyone to really <b>know</b> him. I liked that not <b>too</b> much was revealed about <b>either</b> of them. So I was able to get to <b>know</b> them at the <b>same</b> time they learned those things about each other.<br><br>Overall, I <b>really</b> liked the story and characters. I am <b>so</b> glad I waited for the second book to be out <b>before</b> reading this one, because the <b>cliffhanger</b> would have killed me. Seriously, what a <b>way</b> to end a book! Now, I <b>can't</b> wait to see what happens! I <b>need</b> it now! So, I'm off to read the next.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844399._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6098756108488108117" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer523391130" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5015833978036325709">This started off slow for me, I enjoyed the pace and style of the writing, However I did feel somewhat disconnected from the characters for the first part of the book. The description of the story had me thinking I was going to be reading the typical rich controlling man meets insecure small town girl, but refreshingly this was not the case.<br/><br/>Laurelyn is funny, pretty and has an easy going nature that I enjoyed in her character, as a female lead she ticked all my boxes not a whiny insecure trait i</span>
  <span id="freeText5015833978036325709" style="display:none">This started off slow for me, I enjoyed the pace and style of the writing, However I did feel somewhat disconnected from the characters for the first part of the book. The description of the story had me thinking I was going to be reading the typical rich controlling man meets insecure small town girl, but refreshingly this was not the case.<br><br>Laurelyn is funny, pretty and has an easy going nature that I enjoyed in her character, as a female lead she ticked all my boxes not a whiny insecure trait in sight.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407691i/796586._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jack's character takes a little longer to figure out and as male lead characters go it sadly wasn't insta -love for me, that being said as the book developed I found myself really enjoying his character. He was caring, considerate but at times possessive and loving.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407691i/796587._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their was a predictability factor about this book that I enjoyed and the chemistry was certainly a bonus.<br>I love nothing more than unexpected love and romance and this book delivered. <br><br>The sub characters I didn't care for too much, but that rarely puts me off a book. A big plus for me was the POV from both leading characters.<br><br>The last 30% of this book was what made it for me, and I can't wait to read book two in the series, their are most certainly unanswered questions and I'm sure book two will live up to its predecessor.<br><br>The official blurb sums this book up nicely.<br><br>Thoroughly enjoyed this read, I connected with the authors style, their was moments of love, romance, unexpected kindness, friendship and hope and secret love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407691i/796588.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4 stars. <br></span>
