              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=reread">reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=rich-hero">rich-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522292949" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10123826069110286994"><b>I really LOVED this book! With all the books out right now about rich, controlling, sexy men, this one is a true standout in my eyes. The more I’ve thought about it over the last week, the more I can truly say that I freaking LOVED it!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407527i/796030._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Jack McLachlan is a rich, powerful, well-known businessman and is one of Australia’s most eligible bachelors. He doesn’t do love. He doesn’t do real relationships. Work is his number one priority. So, to keep things simple for him, he enters into intimate arrangeme</span>
  <span id="freeText10123826069110286994" style="display:none"><b>I really LOVED this book! With all the books out right now about rich, controlling, sexy men, this one is a true standout in my eyes. The more I’ve thought about it over the last week, the more I can truly say that I freaking LOVED it!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407527i/796030._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jack McLachlan is a rich, powerful, well-known businessman and is one of Australia’s most eligible bachelors. He doesn’t do love. He doesn’t do real relationships. Work is his number one priority. So, to keep things simple for him, he enters into intimate arrangements with one woman at a time for a set amount of weeks, no strings attached, no one gets hurt. Instead of weeks this time, he’s looking for months, so his decision about who is more important than ever. The question is who’s the lucky woman? After having no luck at a local Australian bar, a beautiful American musician catches his eye at the last second. Jack is immediately intrigued by Laurelyn Prescott and is determined to make her his, at least for a few months.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Her voice is raspy and sexy, her eyes closed. She oozes eroticism. She tilts her head and opens her eyes when she begins to sing the chorus. I swear it feels like she’s looking right in my direction, singing to me.”<br><br>“She has bewitched me. And I want her. She’s the one.”</b>
</i><br><br>As part of Jack’s arrangement, Laurelyn isn’t allowed to know his real name so he has her call him Lachlan. Laurelyn being the strong, stubborn woman that she is decides he doesn’t get to know hers if she can’t know his, so she becomes known as Paige to him. The point of view switches back and forth between Jack and Laurelyn, which I absolutely loved. It worked really well for the story too. It is really helpful throughout the book because we can see Laurelyn’s more vulnerable side that she tries not to show Jack. We also get to see how much Jack truly cares for her. <br><br><i>
  <b>“If I do this, something will go wrong and this man will hurt me. I know it as sure as I’m sitting here next to him feeling how much he makes me want to say yes.”</b>
</i><br><br>The characters are absolutely phenomenal! Laurelyn is my favorite type of heroine. She is down to earth, stubborn, independent, and witty. I felt like she was really smart too, she isn’t trying to play games, but she is definitely aware that her arrangement with Jack isn’t a real relationship. I’m glad there wasn’t a lot of whining in her head and going back and forth about Jack, it would have been easy to go there, but it never did. Georgia Cates was able to build Laurelyn into a really strong character with just enough vulnerability that she is hard not to love. Plus, she was pretty hilarious at times and wasn’t afraid to tease Jack and keep him on his toes. The part where she messes with him about her age was priceless. <br><br>Then of course there is Jack. Oh, Jack McLachlan… I really grew to love this guy! At first I liked him okay and was thinking he was just another gorgeous, rich bachelor. I thought I had him pegged as being somewhat cold and controlling, but he surprised me. Although he does have his boundaries, he has true feelings for Laurelyn and I’m not talking about on a romantic level. Just good feelings, he genuinely cares for her and cares what is going on with her. He worries about her and those parts are oh so very swoon-worthy! That was seriously refreshing! <br><br><i>
  <b>”This man will be hazardous for my heart if I allow it. He’ll use me up if I let him. I know this without a doubt and remind myself of a lesson well learned not so long ago. Never confuse sex for love. Right now, we’re black and white, but I vow that the second it becomes a hazy shade of cold steel gray, I will get out. No question about it.“ </b>
</i> <br><br>…<br><br><i><b>”Why would you doubt me?” <br>“Because I don’t know you.” </b><br>Wow, that hurt. <br><b>“But you’re wrong. Maybe you don’t know my real name, but you know me like no one else does.” </b></i><br><br>I completely fell for the two of them together. I enjoyed the way they interacted and I freaking loved the Aussie lingo in the book… sanger, brekkie, coldie, chickie babe, sunnies! So much awesome! :) The chemistry between the two is also off the charts hot and it had just the right amount of steaminess! As the story progresses, things happen and events lead to revelations between Jack and Laurelyn. The whole time you are wondering when or even if they will develop loving feelings and how that may change their arrangement. I enjoyed every second of their journey and them figuring it all out. <br><br><i><b>“I don’t think you know how good you are at this.” <br>“What am I good at?” <br>“Whatever this is we’re doing.”</b><br>I no longer have any idea what we we’re doing. I only know I like it. <br><b>“I think you’re pretty good at this too. Whatever it is.” </b></i><br><br>The story does end on a bit of a cliffhanger in case you are wondering. Although I was a mess at the end, it wasn’t really because of the cliffhanger. I just felt like I was really getting attached to the characters and I was feeling everything they were. The ending was expected for me, so I was okay with the cliffy. It gives just enough to leave us with some idea of the direction the next book may take. Plus, book #2 – Beauty from Surrender comes out May 30th, that’s not too bad… I’m really excited for it though!<br><br><i>
  <b>“I’ve known pain my whole life, but this is a new kind for me. It isn’t born of something wrong or ugly. This pain is conceived out of beauty…”</b>
</i><br><br>For more reviews go to <a href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Reality Bites! Let's Get Lost!!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10123826069110286994" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</a><br><br>When Laurelyn decides to take a three month vacation with her friend Addison to Australia, she thought the time away from her budding music career and recent break-up with a married boyfriend would be good for her. She's at open mic night at a club and Jack McLachlan sets eyes on her. He's an uber rich wine mogul and prefers his "relationships" as an agreement. An agreement of a set time, no personal information or attachments and when their time is up....they go their separate ways. He's been burned before. He doesn't need some stalker when things get cold. <br><br>So Jack finagles a way to bump into Laurelyn at a vintage dinner. He asks her to dance then subsequently asks her out. At this date he proposes she be his number 13- the woman he will wine, dine, share oodles of time with both in bed and out but nothing personal shall be shared. She is not to know his net worth, his family, friends, or even his name. He promises her the time of her life and when 3 months are up....they go their separate ways. It's obvious he's loaded and is ready to rock her world. <br><br>What neither of them bank on is their feelings begin to grow. They gradually let each other "in." Laurelyn begins to know Jack (aka Lachlen) better than anyone. They've got no pressure...it's just the two of them. Things just bloom. <br><br>But three months quickly arrives and can these two simply walk away from the feelings both of them know they possess?<br><br>As I said, loved the book. It had a shit-ton of angsty suspense I thrive on. I immediately swooned over Jack. Laurelyn has been dealt a fair share of crap in her lifetime but she's a pretty solid, tough heroine. Even if her toughness made me want to SHOOT HER in the end. The book had a fair share of steamy scenes in the bedroom but I'm still wondering why it was tagged BDSM. There is NO BDSM in this book. Just a lot of bow chicka wow wow. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/2477a1e5cbf6abc8708a07b874ae4766_zps3b724ed1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_523839110" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/523839110" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/523839110?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17337340-beauty-from-pain">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-faves-book-1">series-faves-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=billionaire">billionaire</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer523839110" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15217292386432869086"><b>God, how I love, love, love this book!!! </b><br/><br/>I must admit, I put off reading it for a bit, figuring it was just another sexy millionaire story, but this little book smacked me across the face with its awesomeness, and I could not get enough!<br/><br/>First off… meet Jack…<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407758i/796830.jpg' width='360' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407758i/796831.jpg' width='360' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I pictured the gorgeous Matt Bomer the entire way through the book, only to discover that that is exactly who the author pictured for him as well, so that just reinforces his utter and absolute sexiness!<br/><br/>OK, so our heroine is Laurelyn, an Amer</span>
  <span id="freeText15217292386432869086" style="display:none"><b>God, how I love, love, love this book!!! </b><br><br>I must admit, I put off reading it for a bit, figuring it was just another sexy millionaire story, but this little book smacked me across the face with its awesomeness, and I could not get enough!<br><br>First off… meet Jack…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407758i/796830.jpg" width="360" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407758i/796831.jpg" width="360" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I pictured the gorgeous Matt Bomer the entire way through the book, only to discover that that is exactly who the author pictured for him as well, so that just reinforces his utter and absolute sexiness!<br><br>OK, so our heroine is Laurelyn, an American on holiday in Australia for three months with her outrageously hilarious best friend, Addison. She is 22, beautiful and incredibly smart and sassy and I loved her instantly. She is an aspiring singer/songwriter and is taking a break from her life back at home, leaving behind a hard life and a bastard ex-boyfriend. <br><br>Jack Henry McLaughlin (God, even his <i>name</i> is hot!), is a multi-millionaire wine magnate. He spies her in a bar on her first night in town and decides that he has to have her. <br><br><i>"She has bewitched me. And I want her. She's the one."</i><br><br>Fiercely protective of his privacy, he only indulges in anonymous, short-term, no-strings, no-fuss relationships, and he manoeuvres a way to meet Laurelyn where he puts forward a proposal that they ‘date’ for the three months of her stay in Australia. They would not learn each other’s names or personal histories, but they would be together in a relationship of sorts, and at the end of the three months they go their separate ways and never see each other again. It doesn’t take too much convincing for Laurelyn to say yes. <br><br><i>His mouth is so close to mine, I feel his warm breath on my lips. “Right now, all I’m thinking about is how I’m going to get you in my bed so I can show you all the ways I can make you come.” <br>Umm … yes, please and thank you.</i><br><br>The relationship works brilliantly for them both. They spend time together, they have fun together, and everything is laid out up front - they dive straight into it with no fear of rejection or expectation. They are both completely honest about everything from the very beginning, so there is no game playing, and no stupid. They accept each other as they are, and are respectful, affectionate, and hot as all hell. Damn, my kindle was steaming at the chemistry between these two, sensational!<br><br>Throughout the story, it is obvious that apart from the mind-blowing sex, Jack and Laurelyn genuinely care for each other, and I loved watching the easy, flirty affection between them develop into more as they both start feelings thing for the other that they never intended. And despite the end looming on their time together, there is no way they can fight what is happening between them. <br><br><i>“I’m sorry for all the secrecy, for making you feel like you weren’t important enough to know the real me. But I’m most sorry because I have fucked you – I don’t know how many times – and never made love to you.”<br>…<br>We’ve shared countless kisses. They were almost always heated and demanding, but this one is entirely different. It tells me things he can’t or won’t say because it goes against everything he intends for our relationship. </i><br><br>I absolutely adore these characters. Laurelyn is refreshingly self-assured with a wicked sense of humour, and brings a sense of fun and playfulness to Jack’s life. Jack is, obviously, sex on a stick, but he’s not an all-out dominant, controlling Alpha. He is confident and possessive, but he is also funny, incredibly caring and protective of Laurelyn, and goes out of his way to make her feel special, never degrading her and, as he promises her in the beginning, he shows her the time of her life. Laurelyn comes as a complete shock to him, and I loved watching her sneak her way into his life and his heart without either of them really realising it. It was a sensational dynamic. <br><br>And if, individually, they are fantastic, together they are just magic! The banter between them is brilliant, and I loved every little moment that they shared together. And even though the attraction was strong from the very beginning, the pacing of the significant little shifts occurring during their time together was perfect, and very realistic, leading to them slowly and inevitably falling for each other. <br><br><i>“Don’t leave. I want you to be with me.”<br>“You’ll have your family.”<br>I swallow before I say the words that will change this relationship forever. “You’re the one I need.”</i><br><br>I was so impressed that Cates was able to give us such an intense and emotional story without the characters resorting to stupid behaviour and unecessary angst that is so common in a lot of books. Jack and Laurelyn both have nastiness in their pasts, and while it played a part in the story, at no stage did it overcome either of them, or cause issues for them. They dealt with everything up front and openly, and it made it all just that much more enjoyable.<br><br>With fantastic writing, the story moves at a great pace and is told in dual POV, alternating at each chapter, so we get to see where both Jack and Laurelyn’s heads are at the whole way through, and it’s AWESOME! I was captivated from the very first page and I laughed, squeed, and swooned my way through the whole book… God, did I swoon! And that ending (yep, another cliffy!) has left me desperate for more!<br><br>An instant favourite, I absolutely loved it - 5 shining stars.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15217292386432869086" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525968502" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525968502?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Any romance fan who likes a hot, emotion packed story</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=keepers">keepers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525968502" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6198160110578381268"><i>Oh when will I learn to pay attention to what my Goodreads friends are so excited about?</i><br/><br/>I could've had the glorious experience of reading this absorbing, emotional trilogy over a year ago, but did I listen? Well, to be fair to myself, I did put it on my "to-buy" shelf...but then I forgot about it. *sigh*<br/><br/>After being totally enthralled with Emma Chase's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18297707.Tangled__Tangled___1_' title='Tangled (Tangled, #1) by Emma Chase' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tangled</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17977710.Twisted__Tangled___2_' title='Twisted (Tangled, #2) by Emma Chase' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twisted</a>, I was having a hard time letting the stories go in my mind, and I was having a difficult time getting interested in anything </span>
  <span id="freeText6198160110578381268" style="display:none"><i>Oh when will I learn to pay attention to what my Goodreads friends are so excited about?</i><br><br>I could've had the glorious experience of reading this absorbing, emotional trilogy over a year ago, but did I listen? Well, to be fair to myself, I did put it on my "to-buy" shelf...but then I forgot about it. *sigh*<br><br>After being totally enthralled with Emma Chase's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18297707.Tangled__Tangled___1_" title="Tangled (Tangled, #1) by Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangled</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17977710.Twisted__Tangled___2_" title="Twisted (Tangled, #2) by Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Twisted</a>, I was having a hard time letting the stories go in my mind, and I was having a difficult time getting interested in anything else that I had on hand. So I started to go through my "to-buy" shelves, seeing if anything with high reader ratings appealed to me. And then I came across this series, reread some of the reviews, and figured this was just the kind of book that could help me get over <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17977710.Twisted__Tangled___2_" title="Twisted (Tangled, #2) by Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Twisted</a>. And oh boy, did it ever!<br><br>There's over <b>2,300!</b> reviews of this book, so I doubt I'll say anything that hasn't already been said. But Oh-my- <i>God</i> did I <b>love</b> this book! I didn't even care that it ended on a cliff-hanger (since I had the other 2 books in the series ready to go). After I recovered from bawling my eyes out (over that letter!) I plunged into book 2 (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314410.Beauty_from_Surrender__Beauty___2_" title="Beauty from Surrender (Beauty, #2) by Georgia Cates" rel="nofollow noopener">Beauty from Surrender</a>).<br><br>So briefly, the plot: Laurelyn Prescott-- 23, beautiful brunette, fresh out of college, from Nashville, aspiring country singer/songwriter, daughter of a self-absorbed mother and never to be acknowledged love-child of a famous country superstar father. Laurelyn has just had a bad break up (<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[with a married record producer <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>) and is traveling to Australia with her best friend to spend the summer at her best friend's brother's apartment. Laurelyn hopes the time away from Nashville will help her get her head on straight and over the disastrous breakup. She has no plans to get romantically involved with anyone while in Australia (despite her friend's hope that she falls for her attractive brother) and wants to just concentrate on her music.<br><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr090/nashville_zpsc2d8f2cc.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395542521i/9012207.png" alt=" photo nashville_zpsc2d8f2cc.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Laurelyn...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr086/laurelyn_zps89cc995b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395541469i/9012012.jpg" alt=" photo laurelyn_zps89cc995b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Enter Jack McLachlan--30, millionaire most eligible bachelor, known for his string of conquests, his sexy good looks, and his vineyards.<br><br><i>Jack Henry...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr086/e4632157-5854-4633-9fe6-5252db8e400e_zps8042277a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395541071i/9011829.jpg" alt=" photo e4632157-5854-4633-9fe6-5252db8e400e_zps8042277a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jack's ready to pick out his next "companion", but this time he's looking for something that lasts a little longer than his typical 3 weeks. If he finds the right woman, perhaps he can go as long as 3 months? He sees Laurelyn singing in a small club in Wagga Wagga (where he's spending the summer, tending to one of his vineyards) and knows he has to have her. Now, if only he can convince her to agree to his unusual propsition--no names exchanged, no personal info revealed, just good times and great sex and no contact or hard feelings when it's over. What woman wouldn't agree to that?:)<br><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr086/d658c1d7-cfd2-4257-ae11-3842275c588f_zps519068a0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395540937i/9011779.jpg" alt=" photo d658c1d7-cfd2-4257-ae11-3842275c588f_zps519068a0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Jack's fancy sportscar...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr086/59fd3c39-6c9f-449c-8f53-99e6b841b8d8_zps34589d95.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395541353i/9011987.jpg" alt=" photo 59fd3c39-6c9f-449c-8f53-99e6b841b8d8_zps34589d95.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The vineyards...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr086/982b5e27-2736-472c-84c7-10cb70a41c5f_zpsaf1f9d11.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395541353i/9011988.png" alt=" photo 982b5e27-2736-472c-84c7-10cb70a41c5f_zpsaf1f9d11.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I won't go beyond that with the plot except to say that Laurelyn eventually agrees, but then makes the mistake of giving her heart to Jack (or Lachlan, as he's told her) and is met with devastating heartbreak. Oh, I bawled my eyes out over the letter she wrote to him...*<i>sniff</i>*<br><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr089/cryinggif_zps7f1d736a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395542176ra/9012142.gif" alt=" photo cryinggif_zps7f1d736a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved these characters!!! I loved the setting, the plot, and the development of the characters. Jack Henry, despite your flaws, I loved you. Luvved you. Laurelyn, I felt your pain, and was rooting for you. Your songs killed me. I loved the supporting characters (especially Jack's family). I couldn't understand Jack's insistence on not ever having a real relationship that included marriage and family (the reason why isn't revealed until the second book) so that was sort of an unanswered question...but any questions I had were answered in the second book, so it all worked out. I would advise anyone interested in this book to have the next two handy, because you're going to want to jump right into them to find out what happens. There's plenty of highs and lows along the way in the series, disagreements, disappointments, and lots and lots of making up and <i>plenty</i> of hot, emotional sex that will leave you swooning...yeah.:)<br><br>I can't recommend this series highly enough. I'm still not over it and haven't read anything in a week. That and the fact that it made me cry makes it a keeper in my book. 5 big stars</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6198160110578381268" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer542967329" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18021939017580560988"><i>
  <b> LOVE LOVE LOVED THIS BOOK !!!! ♥♥ </b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>Jack Henry and Laurelyn</b>
</i><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>I'm so sad that this ones finished and I have to wait till May for the sequel. This book totally owned me from page 1.. everything about it! The chemistry between Jack and Laurelyn was so good and I just loved them together. I don't know exactly what is was in particular about this couple that affected me so strongly... I've read plenty of love stories, epic love stories, other stories with possibly more romance but s</span>
  <span id="freeText18021939017580560988" style="display:none"><i>
  <b> LOVE LOVE LOVED THIS BOOK !!!! ♥♥ </b>
</i><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Jack Henry and Laurelyn</b>
</i><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>I'm so sad that this ones finished and I have to wait till May for the sequel. This book totally owned me from page 1.. everything about it! The chemistry between Jack and Laurelyn was so good and I just loved them together. I don't know exactly what is was in particular about this couple that affected me so strongly... I've read plenty of love stories, epic love stories, other stories with possibly more romance but something about them was just different.. I love the back and forth pov's so we were able to see what each of them were thinking and feeling.. maybe thats part of what got me so emotionally attached to them. <br><br>Jack and Laurelyn meet and its instant attraction.. Jack Henry convinces her to be his for the 3 months that she is on vaca in Austraila. He does not even want them to exchange their real names.. he's a multi-millionair that owns several wine vineyards.... he doesnt want attachments.. he wants his women to have no idea who he is so he can use them and toss them aside when he's done and does not want them to be able to find him when its over.. these "relationships" are set in stone from the start with just a few weeks time period. Something about Laurelyn has him wanting the whole 3 months she is there.. so Jack Henry take her to one of his Vineyards..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380885589i/3142015.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>As the weeks progress.. of course feelings get stronger.. Laurelyn has fallen head over heels in love with Jack Henry but she knows this is only a temporary arrangment.. she hopes that he feels the same and that he will ask her to stay.. if only he could love her back. Will he? <br><br>Can't wait for book 2.... I know I will re-read this one again right before it comes out so that I can expierence them again from the beginning....<br><br><i>I’ve known pain my whole life, but this is a new kind for me. It isn’t born of something wrong or ugly. This pain is conceived out of beauty— my love for Jack Henry McLachlan. I embrace it. I clutch it as tightly as I can with both fists because I never want to forget the love I have for him. Loving him will forever be my Beauty from Pain.</i><br><br><br><span>[image error]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="18021939017580560988" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_523268818" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/523268818" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/523268818?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=steamy-reads">steamy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=contracts-and-arrangements">contracts-and-arrangements</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=rich-guy-hero">rich-guy-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=alternate-pov">alternate-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=female-rock-star">female-rock-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=say-it-with-music">say-it-with-music</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer523268818" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer394344827101675443"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407670i/796514._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407670i/796515._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So, I finished this book when I was working away and therefore, went straight onto book two. So I'm writing this review whilst I am halfway through the second book, which is something I try to avoid doing.<br/><br/>Firstly, I'm really really loving this series. When I first started <i>Beauty from Pain</i> I wasn't sure it was going to be for me. But then, I've been through a real run of books that haven't floated my boat, so I was beginning to wonder if I was needing some time away from my beloved Kindle. <br/><br/>Howeve</span>
  <span id="freeText394344827101675443" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407670i/796514._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407670i/796515._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I finished this book when I was working away and therefore, went straight onto book two. So I'm writing this review whilst I am halfway through the second book, which is something I try to avoid doing.<br><br>Firstly, I'm really really loving this series. When I first started <i>Beauty from Pain</i> I wasn't sure it was going to be for me. But then, I've been through a real run of books that haven't floated my boat, so I was beginning to wonder if I was needing some time away from my beloved Kindle. <br><br>However, <i>Beauty from Pain</i> pulled me out of my slump! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The pain is conceived out of beauty - my love for Jack Henry McLachlan. I embrace it. I clutch it as tightly as I can with both fists because I never want to forget the love I have for him. Loving him will forever be my Beauty from Pain.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Knowing I had to get up for work at 4am, I couldn't force myself to put Jack Henry and Laurelyn down until I'd finished the book at 2am! Cue a very sleepy, very clumsy, <i>very</i> grouchy Smitten. Oops!<br><br>I loved the will they/won't they throughout this book... will they reveal their real identity, will they admit to falling in love, will he ask her to stay... Aaargh! Scrummy!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You don't always know the true worth of a woman's love until it becomes a memory."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Jack Henry, and the sex scenes, are haaawt! We all love a sexy multi-millionaire... and now we have a sexy <i>secret</i> multi-millionaire, with a filthy mouth and an Australian accent!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Right now, all I'm thinking about is how I'm going to get you in my bed so I can show you all the ways I can make you come."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Laurelyn takes a trip to Australia, with best friend Addison, for the Christmas holidays, to escape a previous relationship-gone-bad. Despite wanting nothing less than to meet a man, she can't help the lure she feels when she bumps into charming, handsome, Aussie 'suit', Jack Henry McLachlan.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407670i/796516.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Jack needs a certain type of relationship. One where identity is kept secret, real names are withheld and contact is forbidden once their three months is up. Of course, Laurelyn agrees and their strange affair begins.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Listen to me, Laurelyn. The best way to get over somebody is to get under someone else."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Laurelyn is a great female lead. She has a playful, real character and isn't afraid to speak her mind. I can't stand miscommunications in books, and I was pleased that these characters seemed able to talk things through, despite the need for secrecy in their relationship.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"How can you think it's possible to have something this hot without one of us getting burned?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book does end in a cliffhanger. I'm really glad that I waited until <i>Beauty from Surrender</i> was released, to read these books as I know this cliffhanger would have irritated me if I hadn't. But now that both books are available, I'd definitely recommend this series, so far!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407670i/796517._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Beauty from Pain</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> Cliffhanger<br><b>Series:</b> ✓ <br><b>Reading Order: </b><br>Book #1 - Beauty from Pain<br>Book #2 - Beauty from Surrender<br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> No<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Rich hero<br>Secret affair<br><b>Warning. This book includes...</b> <br>Graphic sexual content<br><b>Writing:</b> Good<br><br>UK AMAZON: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Beauty-From-Pain-Series/dp/148234873X/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1372598668&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=beauty+from+pain">http://www.amazon.co.uk/Beauty-From-P...</a><br>US AMAZON: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Beauty-From-Pain-Series/dp/148234873X/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1372598668&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=beauty+from+pain">http://www.amazon.com/Beauty-From-Pai...</a><br><br><b>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/629301464?book_show_action=true">May 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer629301464" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9270605510282612625"><b>Why the cliffhanger?!</b> Why, why, why, why, why?<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406152ra/792044.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Jack Henry McLachlan, I could just punch you in the face! <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423608ra/844010.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423608ra/844011.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Ooo, wait I know the answer!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418085ra/827564.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/380344.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*calm down now, Destini*</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401963ra/780771.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>All that out now, I can say that this was a great, <b>entertaining</b> read. The writing was great, Jack was just <b>scrumptious</b>, and there was a <b>kick ass heroine. </b><br/><br/>Jack:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423608i/844012._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Laurelyn:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423608i/844013._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>After getting her heart torn out, Laurelyn Prescott decides she needs a change of scenery. As in, the other side of the world. So, for three months Laurelyn and her friend, Add</span>
  <span id="freeText9270605510282612625" style="display:none"><b>Why the cliffhanger?!</b> Why, why, why, why, why?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406152ra/792044.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Jack Henry McLachlan, I could just punch you in the face! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423608ra/844010.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423608ra/844011.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ooo, wait I know the answer!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418085ra/827564.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/380344.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*calm down now, Destini*</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401963ra/780771.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All that out now, I can say that this was a great, <b>entertaining</b> read. The writing was great, Jack was just <b>scrumptious</b>, and there was a <b>kick ass heroine. </b><br><br>Jack:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423608i/844012._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Laurelyn:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423608i/844013._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>After getting her heart torn out, Laurelyn Prescott decides she needs a change of scenery. As in, the other side of the world. So, for three months Laurelyn and her friend, Addison, will be staying in Australia.<br>Jack McLachlan is good-looking, rich, and one of the most eligible bachelors. But he isn’t looking for a relationship. At least, not one that'll last more than three months. <br>Laurelyn and Jack start their affair complete with aliases, a three month expiration date, and a no contact rule once it’s finished. <br>However, they never planned on falling in love. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “You might as well be the devil.”<br>“Baby, you’re the one holding the apple.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>First things first, Laurelyn:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/431655.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>By far, one of my favorite heroines. I don’t have a single complaint. She was smart, sassy, and completely real. <br>With these types of stories, I’m always afraid that once they start to have feelings and the time comes that they have to leave, they’ll make a pathetic scene or pretend that this was new information. <br>Laurelyn was not like that <b>at all.</b> She always knew why she was there. She didn’t conveniently forget or try to look for something that wasn’t there. She held on to her <b>dignity.</b><br><i>
  <blockquote> I didn’t love you the day I met you, or even a month later. But somewhere between hello and the goodbye I’m unable to bear, I fell desperately in love with you.</blockquote>
</i><br><br>Jack just stole my heart. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/475397.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was a little unsure one whether or not I was going to like him because, frankly, he was a boring in the beginning. Now, I’m naming our children. He was totally swoon-worthy. <s>Except when he was being the world’s biggest moron.</s><br><br><i>Beauty From Pain</i> is told in alternating POV’s which was fantastic because you were able to see where their head’s where at. It also helped me become closer and build a connection with both of them.<br><br>Even though their relationship (if you could call it that) was pretty much a lie, it felt so <b>real.</b> They were so good together. Jack was guarded and reserved in the beginning, but with Laurelyn’s help, he opened up. <br><br>Now, on to book two where, hopefully, Jack has gotten his head out of his ass because right now, this face:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417821ra/826793.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>is not amused.<br><br><i>
  <blockquote> I’ve known pain my whole life, but this is a new kind for me. It isn’t born of something wrong or ugly. This pain is conceived out of beauty– my love for Jack Henry McLachlan. </blockquote>
</i></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525227043?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog by: </span>
      Trish 
  </div>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525227043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8633924617281608563">Five Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>I’m on the ledge, about to fall. Or jump. I’m not sure which, and then I hear his possessive words through gritted teeth and it sends me over the edge. “No one else touches you. Only me. Do you understand?” </i>
</b><br/><br/>FUCK. That was so unbelievably good. Wow. Just wow. <br/><br/>I wanted to read this for a long time, but I knew this was going to end in a cliffhanger, so I waited for the sequel to come out. So when it finally did, I no longer had any excuses not to; I dove right in. I cannot believe how</span>
  <span id="freeText8633924617281608563" style="display:none">Five Stars<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I’m on the ledge, about to fall. Or jump. I’m not sure which, and then I hear his possessive words through gritted teeth and it sends me over the edge. “No one else touches you. Only me. Do you understand?” </i>
</b><br /><br />FUCK. That was so unbelievably good. Wow. Just wow. <br /><br />I wanted to read this for a long time, but I knew this was going to end in a cliffhanger, so I waited for the sequel to come out. So when it finally did, I no longer had any excuses not to; I dove right in. I cannot believe how good this was. I haven’t read an actual five-star read in such a long time; this totally relieved that ache. It had everything I craved in a book: A strong Alpha male Hero (who by the way has a sexy Australian accent --- which made me create a new shelf <i>I love Aussies</i> LOL!), sizzling sex and just a touch of angst. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I can’t wait to have a naughty with you. You know it’s only a matter of time, and when I do, I’m going to make you come so hard.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Jack McLachlan is looking for his next conquest, one that will share his bed for the next few months. His past <i>conquests</i> have only lasted three to four weeks at best, but this time, he wants it a little more prolonged. He doesn’t do relationships. He’s a very rich man and the women he use to date wanted more from him. He’s learned his lesson: Be upfront, no telling of real names, no falling in love, just sex, lots of sex, and afterwards, make a clean break. Simple. <br /><br />When he spots Laurelyn, he immediately knew his search was over. When he finds out she’s only in Australia for a few months, he knew it was meant to be. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“No. I can’t love a lie and that’s all we were.” </i>
</b><br /><br />When Laurelyn landed in Australia to visit her best friend’s brother, she did not expect to meet a man like Jack. She immediately dismisses Jack’s initial <i>proposal</i>, but couldn’t help but be curious. She decides to live and dive into this arrangement with Jack. She doesn’t know anything about this man, not even his name. What she does find out is that Jack is willing to make all her fantasies come true. She knows she’s living in a fantasy and that it comes with an expiration date, but sooner or later the balloon is going to burst on the fantasy and real feelings start to emerge from both her and Jack. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>I love her too much to let her leave and I need to tell her right this minute.</i>
</b><br /><br />Laurelyn is unlike any of his past companions. He doesn’t know what to do. He wants more time with this southern belle, but his constant state of denial keeps him from really opening up to her. All Laurelyn wanted was some sort of reassurance of his feelings, but will it come too late? As I read this, a ticking clock was always in the background. I was constantly on the edge of my seat wondering how these two will pull this off. <br /><br />I loved everything about this story and I’m happy that book two is immediately available to me because that ending was simply unacceptable. OMG! I need a resolution NOW! Loved this story! <br /><br />-----<br />Me, prior to having the sequel out LOL:<br /><br />UGH! Once again, I was all set to read this, then BAM! Found out it ends in a cliffhanger. <b>CURSE YOU, CLIFFHANGERS!!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8633924617281608563" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_488705874" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/488705874" />
    <a title="Kirsty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10389044-kirsty"><img alt="Kirsty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1409522343p2/10389044.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/488705874?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirsty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirsty" href="/user/show/10389044-kirsty">Kirsty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10389044-kirsty?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer488705874" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer409501786658452260">I am so blown away by this book that I'm not even sure how to put it in to words, but I guess I'll try..<br/><br/>Beauty from Pain is so unlike anything else I have ever read. Yes we may have the broken heroine who is struggling to deal with a painful break up, and we may have the sexy billionaire, but apart from that everything else is so new.<br/><br/>Laurelyn Prescott is embarking on a three month trip around the world to Australia with her best friend, Addison. They will be staying with Addison's brother and fo</span>
  <span id="freeText409501786658452260" style="display:none">I am so blown away by this book that I'm not even sure how to put it in to words, but I guess I'll try..<br><br>Beauty from Pain is so unlike anything else I have ever read. Yes we may have the broken heroine who is struggling to deal with a painful break up, and we may have the sexy billionaire, but apart from that everything else is so new.<br><br>Laurelyn Prescott is embarking on a three month trip around the world to Australia with her best friend, Addison. They will be staying with Addison's brother and forgetting about life back home. Just what Laurelyn needs - a break, the sun, a bit of fun with her best friend and NO men. With some wise words from Addison, their journey begins.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Listen to me, Laurelyn. The best way to get over somebody is to get under someone else."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Jack McLachlan. Jack freaking McLahlan. I absolutely loved him. He was the rich and sexy billionaire owner of many wineries across Australia and New Zealand but he doesn't like the world, or his 'companions' to know this. He is a mystery to woman and that is exactly the way he intends to keep it when he meets Laurelyn one night in a bar. <br><br>They agree on 3 months together. Nothing more, nothing less. This is perfect for both Jack and Laurelyn, Jack because he doesn't have time in his life for more and Laurelyn because she will be returning home to the US after this 3 months and will never have to see him again. It's all very simple, 3 months, no sharing personal details of each others lives - including names, and by the end of it they will both walk away never seeing each other again. Easy, right? I'll let you find out...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Baby, you've fucked my mind without touching my body."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>This was one of the sexiest books I have ever read, but there was so much more to it than just the hot and steamy scenes. I felt real, heavy emotions whilst reading this. All the way through I was almost pleading and begging Jack to just give in and say to hell with his three months and I was never sure whether I was going to get my way or not. It does leave off in a cliffhanger but thankfully we are given the first chapter of the next book, due out May 20th, so you can definitely see the direction the book will be taking. I can not wait to get back to some more of Laurelyn and Jack. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Loving him will forever be my Beauty from Pain.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402514ra/782419.gif" width="399" height="223" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="409501786658452260" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_525450504" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/525450504" />
    <a title="Tessa Teevan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10602787-tessa-teevan"><img alt="Tessa Teevan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604514740p2/10602787.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/525450504?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessa Teevan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessa Teevan" href="/user/show/10602787-tessa-teevan">Tessa Teevan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10602787-tessa-teevan?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer525450504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12219454489992866576">My Jack Henry!!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407993i/797587._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/>Jack Henry McLachlan, a wealthy wine magnate and one of Australia's most notorious bachelors, is a man who doesn't do relationships, and he certainly never falls in love. Jack does anonymous, casual sex, and he's looking for his next fling. <br/><br/>American musician Laurelyn Prescott is spending the next three months in Australia with her best friend, Addison. Jack becomes enchanted with her when he witnesses her singing at a bar on her first night in Australia. She's beautiful, breathta</span>
  <span id="freeText12219454489992866576" style="display:none">My Jack Henry!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407993i/797587._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>Jack Henry McLachlan, a wealthy wine magnate and one of Australia's most notorious bachelors, is a man who doesn't do relationships, and he certainly never falls in love. Jack does anonymous, casual sex, and he's looking for his next fling. <br><br>American musician Laurelyn Prescott is spending the next three months in Australia with her best friend, Addison. Jack becomes enchanted with her when he witnesses her singing at a bar on her first night in Australia. She's beautiful, breathtaking, and best of all, she'll be thousands of miles away when he's done with her. <br><br>After a quick encounter at the bar, and another at a local wine event, Laurelyn agrees to go to dinner with Jack. Jack uses this date to extend his proposition to Laurelyn: They're together exclusively for the next three months, they use aliases, and at the end, they part ways without another glance. Initially, Laurelyn immediately says no. Hell no. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/458038.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jack, not one to give up that easily, tells her to think about it and if she changes her mind, she can meet him the next evening. <br><br><i>
  <b>If you say yes, you'd spend the next three months having the time of your life.</b>
</i><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407993ra/797588.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The more she thinks about it, the more fascinated Laurelyn is with the idea. Addison is quick to push her to accept. <i>
  <b>Umm, the best three months of your life and fantasties coming true? It's a no brainer.</b>
</i> Laurelyn accepts his proposal, with neither of them realizing that this relationship will end up like neither of them expected. <br><br>Over time, they both realize that this physical, no emotions relationship isn't enough, and they both are struggling to fight the rising feelings that have developed over time. As they continue to spend their days and nights together, they inadvertently begin to learn more and more about each other, making it even harder to fight their feelings.<br><br>Their time goes by all too quickly, and eventually it's time for Laurelyn to head back to the States. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407993ra/797589.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's all good, right? This is exactly what Laurelyn signed up for, and exactly what Jack wanted. This is what was meant to be, right? Or have they invaded each other's hearts in such a way that saying goodbye is devastatingly impossible?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407993i/797590.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To put it plain and simply, I loved this book. I was pleasantly surprised with dual POVs. It was thrilling hearing Jack's side of things as his relationship with Laurelyn progressed. I loved and admired Laurelyn's strength. Even once she realized her feelings were growing, she was strong enough to accept that Jack hadn't signed up for that. I did want to shake her a bit once it was so obvious that he was head over heels for her. <br><br>The bedroom/bathroom/gym/pool scenes are some of the steamiest I've read in a while. Both Jack and Laurelyn are extremely passionate, sexual individuals and they simply ignite when they touch. Their sexual chemistry, their chemistry in general, is explosive. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/419747.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book ends in a cliffhanger in the utmost heartbreaking fashion, and days later, I can't stop thinking about Jack Henry and Laurelyn. I need part 2 NOW!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/512044.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12219454489992866576" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4TqXhP2/NH5DAZ1ZWIlsKPXfkqaT1FzLLYGK6Z7o+SZKVOvOeW32Fs+PsWy14JjGRQJIdZ5s6Md13W2MjUjLhg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VOvmsdAOUtMEniIWwNGD+w1a+vZ1W+tbr6ug+A3KTI3/hZr7VNyQu4gQDiMtuHcVvYcgJXjjX1f390edHmp+LQ==')})
  }
